hagia_sophia = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 151

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 537.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 2

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = miaphysite
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_global_flag = hagia_sophia_now_mosque
			}
			show_ambient_object = hagia_sophia_minarets
		}
		else = {
			show_ambient_object = hagia_sophia
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = hagia_sophia_minarets
		hide_ambient_object = hagia_sophia
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = miaphysite
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = miaphysite
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = catholic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_religious_conversion_resistance = 0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_development_cost = 0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			tolerance_own = 1
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.01
			monthly_piety = 0.001
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 7000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_religious_conversion_resistance = 0.2
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_development_cost = 0.2
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
            global_missionary_strength = 0.002
			tolerance_own = 2
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.02
			monthly_piety = 0.002
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 20
				}
			}
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 960
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 14000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_culture_conversion_cost = -0.3
			local_religious_conversion_resistance = 0.3
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		    local_missionary_maintenance_cost = -0.3
			local_development_cost = 0.3
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
            global_missionary_strength = 0.003
			tolerance_own = 3
			yearly_patriarch_authority = 0.03
			tolerance_heathen = 3
			monthly_piety = 0.003
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 30
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

stonehenge = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 7420

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = -2500.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 2

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = pagan
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = stonehenge
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = stonehenge
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = pagan
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = pagan
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		    local_manpower_modifier = 0.10
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_hostile_movement_speed = 0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			leader_land_shock = 1
			hostile_attrition = 1
			shock_damage = 0.10
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
	
	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 7000

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier

	tier_3 = {

tower_of_london = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 236

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1078.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 7

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				culture = normand
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = tower_of_london
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = tower_of_london
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				culture = normand
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1774
		OR = {
			AND = {
				culture = normand
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
			AND = {
				culture = english
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.1
			
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			hostile_disembark_speed = 0.3
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			naval_morale = 0.1
			shock_damage_received = -0.1
			own_coast_naval_combat_bonus = 1.0
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {

		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier

buddha_statues = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 2225

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 570.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	type = monument

	build_trigger = {

				religion = vajrayana

			}

				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

		show_ambient_object = buddha_small
		show_ambient_object = buddha_big

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_small
		hide_ambient_object = buddha_big

				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana

				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes

	}

kremlin = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 6975

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1339.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_slavic
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = kremlin
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = kremlin
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		culture_group = east_slavic
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?

	    is_year = 1849

	}

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		culture = inca
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = machu_picchu
	}

	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = machu_picchu

	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		culture = inca

moai = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 1988

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1400.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		culture = polynesian
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = moai
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = moai
	}

	#can our country use it?

		culture = polynesian
	}

	    always = no
		#culture = polynesian

	}

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1325.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 3

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		culture_group = central_american

			has_owner_culture = yes

		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = tenochtitlan
	}

shwedagon_pagoda = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 4399

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1362.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = shwedagon_pagoda
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = shwedagon_pagoda
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1775
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_unrest = -0.5
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
	
	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_unrest = -0.75
			local_development_cost = -0.05
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
			monthly_karma = 0.05
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 10
				}
			}
		}
	}

the_grand_palace = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 4831

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1782.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 2

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1782
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = dharmic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

jokhang_temple = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 677

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 647.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 2

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = jokhang_temple
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = jokhang_temple
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
	    always = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {

			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)

borobudur_temple = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 2690

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 750.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 3

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = javanese
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = borobudur_temple
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = borobudur_temple
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = javanese
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
	    always = no
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = buddhism
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = vajrayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion = mahayana
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				culture = javanese
				OR = {
					has_owner_culture = yes
					has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

temple_of_confucius = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 2140

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 1302.01.01 #Yuan Dynasty restoration

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 1

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		religion = confucianism
		has_owner_religion = yes
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
		show_ambient_object = temple_of_confucius
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = temple_of_confucius
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		religion = confucianism
		has_owner_religion = yes
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1530
		religion = confucianism
		has_owner_religion = yes
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)

		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			yearly_harmony = 0.25
			religious_unity = 0.25
			prestige = 0.25
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			owner = {
				add_estate_loyalty = {
					estate = estate_church
					loyalty = 5
				}
			}
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)

			months = 240

	move_days_per_unit_distance = 1

	starting_tier = 1

	type = monument

	    is_year = 1225

walls_of_theodosius = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 7137

	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = 450.01.01

	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}

	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0

	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no

	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10

	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 3

	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = christian
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
	}

	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
		hide_ambient_object = walls_of_theodosius
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = christian
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion_group = christian
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		    local_defensiveness = 0.25
			local_hostile_attrition = 2.5
			local_unrest = -2.5
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier

plaza_de_armas = {
    start = 808
    
    date = 1534.01.01
    
    time = {
        months = 0
    }
    
    build_cost = 0
    
    can_be_moved = no
    
    move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
    
    starting_tier = 1
    
    type = monument

    build_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1534
        culture_group = iberian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}		
    }

    on_built = {
    }
    
    on_destroyed = {
    }

    can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
	    culture_group = iberian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}	
    }

    can_upgrade_trigger = {
		culture_group = iberian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}	
    }

    keep_trigger = {
    }

    tier_0 = {
        upgrade_time = {
            months = 0
        }

        cost_to_upgrade = {
            factor = 0
        }

        province_modifiers = {
        }

        area_modifier = {
        }

        country_modifiers = {
        }

        on_upgraded = {
        }
    }

    tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			army_tradition = 0.25
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
}

plaza_del_zocalo = {
    start = 852
    
    date = 1521.01.01
    
    time = {
        months = 0
    }
    
    build_cost = 0
    
    can_be_moved = no
    
    move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
    
    starting_tier = 1
    
    type = monument

    build_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1521
        culture_group = iberian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}		
    }

    on_built = {
    }
    
    on_destroyed = {
    }

    can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
	    culture_group = iberian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}	
    }

    can_upgrade_trigger = {
		culture_group = iberian
		OR = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		}	
    }

    keep_trigger = {
    }

    tier_0 = {
        upgrade_time = {
            months = 0
        }

        cost_to_upgrade = {
            factor = 0
        }

        province_modifiers = {
        }

        area_modifier = {
        }

        country_modifiers = {
        }

        on_upgraded = {
        }
    }

    tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 120
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 3000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			army_tradition = 0.25
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.25
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			army_tradition = 0.25
			prestige = 0.25
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}
}

    }

		}

		}

			local_defensiveness = 0.25
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier

		}

	}

	tier_2 = {

		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 5000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier

		OR = {
			AND = {

			}

				religion = coptic

			}

				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			AND = {
				religion = orthodox
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND = {
				religion = coptic
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
			AND= {
				religion_group = muslim
				has_owner_religion = yes
			}
		}
	}

    keep_trigger = {
    }

    tier_0 = {
        upgrade_time = {
            months = 0

        cost_to_upgrade = {
            factor = 0
        }

        province_modifiers = {
        }

        area_modifier = {
        }

        country_modifiers = {

        }

	start = 7833	#Approximate
	
	# date built in real life
	date = 1000.1.1
	
	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 24
	}
	
	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 250
	
	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = yes
	
	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	
	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 0	#Temple destroyed by Teutonic Order during their expansion into Prussia
	
	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			religion = baltic_pagan_reformed
		}
		AND = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			culture_group = baltic
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
	
	}
	
	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
	
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			religion = baltic_pagan_reformed
		}
		AND = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			culture_group = baltic
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			religion = baltic_pagan_reformed
		}
		AND = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			culture_group = baltic
		}	
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
		FROM = { religion = baltic_pagan_reformed }
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 60
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 400
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			trade_value = 0.25
			local_monthly_devastation = -0.025
			local_unrest = -1
			local_missionary_strength = -0.005
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_religious_conversion_resistance = 0.75
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.025
			tolerance_own = 0.5
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			7834 = {
				change_religion = baltic_pagan_reformed
			}
			7836 = {
				change_religion = baltic_pagan_reformed
			}
		}
	}
	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			trade_value_modifier = 0.05
			trade_goods_size = 0.5
			trade_value = 0.5
			local_monthly_devastation = -0.05
			local_unrest = -2
			local_missionary_strength = -0.01
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_unrest = -0.5
			local_religious_conversion_resistance = 0.90
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.05
			church_influence_modifier = 0.025
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.025
			warscore_cost_vs_other_religion = -0.05
			land_morale = 0.025
			tolerance_own = 1
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			7833 = {
				ROOT = {
					infantry = PREV
				}
				ROOT = {
					infantry = PREV
				}
				ROOT = {
					infantry = PREV
				}
				ROOT = {
					infantry = PREV
				}
				ROOT = {
					cavalry = PREV
				}
			}
		}
	}

	tier_3 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 7000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			trade_value_modifier = 0.1
			trade_goods_size = 0.5
			trade_value = 1
			local_monthly_devastation = -0.07
			local_unrest = -3
			local_missionary_strength = -0.025
			local_regiment_cost = -0.1
			local_defensiveness = 0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			trade_value_modifier = 0.05
			local_manpower_modifier = 0.1
			local_unrest = -1
			local_religious_conversion_resistance = 1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			church_loyalty_modifier = 0.075
			church_influence_modifier = 0.05
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.05
			warscore_cost_vs_other_religion = -0.10
			land_morale = 0.5
			missionaries = 1
			global_missionary_strength = 0.02
			tolerance_own = 2
			shock_damage_received = -0.10
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			add_base_tax = 3
			add_base_production = 3
			add_base_manpower = 3
		}
	}
}

warsaw_castle = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 257		#Warsaw
	
	# date built in real life
	date = 1313.6.1		#Original fort built in 1313 but significantly expanded around 1410
	
	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 24
	}
	
	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 500
	
	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no
	
	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	
	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 0	#Probably not significant enough in 1444 to start as tier 1
	
	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			is_capital = yes
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
	
	}
	
	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
	
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			is_capital = yes
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		OR = {
			FROM = { tag = MAZ }
			is_year = 1598		#Capital moved to Warsaw
		}
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			is_capital = yes
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}	
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
		has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
		has_owner_religion = yes
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic
				culture_group = south_slavic
				culture_group = east_slavic
			}
		}
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 60
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 400
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			trade_value_modifier = 0.075
			local_defensiveness = 0.05
			local_unrest = -0.5
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			improve_relation_modifier = 0.2
			prestige_decay = -0.005
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			add_prestige = 5
		}
	}
	
	tier_2 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 240
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1500
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			local_defensiveness = 0.05
			local_unrest = -1
			local_development_cost = -0.05
			statewide_governing_cost = -0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			local_tax_modifier = 0.05
			local_build_cost = -0.025
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			improve_relation_modifier = 0.3
			governing_capacity = 50
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.025
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			add_prestige = 5
			add_splendor = 50
		}
	}
	
	tier_3 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 480
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 8000
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {
			trade_value_modifier = 0.1
			local_defensiveness = 0.15
			local_unrest = -1
			local_development_cost = -0.075
			statewide_governing_cost = -0.2
			local_state_maintenance_modifier = -0.1
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
			trade_value_modifier = 0.02
			local_development_cost = -0.025
			local_tax_modifier = 0.1
			local_build_cost = -0.05
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
			improve_relation_modifier = 0.3
			prestige_decay = -0.0025
			governing_capacity = 75
			stability_cost_modifier = -0.05
			diplomatic_reputation = 1
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
			add_base_tax = 2
			add_base_production = 2
			add_base_manpower = 2
			add_prestige = 5
		}
	}
}

tre_kronor = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 1		#Paradox HQ
	
	# date built in real life
	date = 1350.1.1		#King named the castle Tre Kronor (good enough?)
	
	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 24
	}
	
	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 500
	
	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no
	
	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	
	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 0
	
	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			culture_group = scandinavian
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					accepted_culture = swedish
					capital = 1
				}
				tag = SWE
				tag = SCA
				tag = NOR
				tag = DAN
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
	
	}
	
	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
	
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			culture_group = scandinavian
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					accepted_culture = swedish
					capital = 1
				}
				tag = SWE
				tag = SCA
				tag = NOR
				tag = DAN
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
	    is_year = 1754		#Date of its reconstruction after being demolished by fire in 1697
		AND = {
			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			culture_group = scandinavian
		}

				tag = NOR
				tag = DAN
			}
		}	
	}

			has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			has_owner_religion = yes
			culture_group = scandinavian
		}
		FROM = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					accepted_culture = swedish
					capital = 1
				}
				tag = SWE

				tag = NOR
				tag = DAN
			}
		}
	}

	#tier data
	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 0
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 0
		}

		province_modifiers = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the provinces in the map area when we have this project here on this tier
		area_modifier = {
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the country when we have this project here on this tier
		country_modifiers = {
		}

		#what effects happen when this tier is achieved
		on_upgraded = {
		}
	}

	tier_1 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		upgrade_time = {
			months = 60
		}

		#cost to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)
		cost_to_upgrade = {
			factor = 1200
		}

		#what modifiers are added to the province when we have this project here on this tier
		province_modifiers = {

		months = 24
	}

	build_cost = 250

	can_be_moved = no
	
	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 10
	
	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 0	#Destroyed during German conquest of Pomerania

	type = monument

		AND = {
			has_owner_culture = yes

		}
		AND = {
			has_owner_culture = yes
			OR = {
				culture_group = west_slavic

				culture_group = east_slavic

		}

lighthouse_of_alexandria = {
	# province it starts in
	start = 358
	
	# date built in real life (so anything built during game time will be there if you start a game after that date)
	date = -280.01.01
	
	#time to build
	time = {
		months = 0
	}
	
	#how much to build one
	build_cost = 0
	
	#can we move it?
	can_be_moved = no
	
	#time to move the project one unit of distance, in days
	move_days_per_unit_distance = 2
	
	#tier that the project starts at when first placed in the game (be that at game start or when built by a country as the game progresses)
	starting_tier = 0	#Destroyed by Crete earthquake in 1303
	
	#project type
	type = monument

	#can we build it?
	build_trigger = {
		adm_tech = 10
		AND = {
			OR = {
				has_owner_culture = yes
				has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			}
			OR = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				culture_group = iranian
				culture_group = egyptian_group
				culture_group = old_latin
				culture_group = latin
				culture = old_egyptian
				culture = al_misr_arabic
			}
		}
	}

	#what to do when it's built
	on_built = {
	}
	
	#what to do when it's destroyed
	on_destroyed = {
	}

	#can our country use it?
	can_use_modifiers_trigger = {
		adm_tech = 10
		AND = {
			OR = {
				has_owner_culture = yes
				has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			}
			OR = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				culture_group = iranian
				culture_group = egyptian_group
				culture_group = old_latin
				culture_group = latin
				culture = old_egyptian
				culture = al_misr_arabic
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country upgrade it?
	can_upgrade_trigger = {
		adm_tech = 10
		AND = {
			OR = {
				has_owner_culture = yes
				has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			}
			OR = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				culture_group = iranian
				culture_group = egyptian_group
				culture_group = old_latin
				culture_group = latin
				culture = old_egyptian
				culture = al_misr_arabic
			}
		}
	}

	#can our country keep it or is it destroyed when we get hold of it?
	keep_trigger = {
		adm_tech = 10
		AND = {
			OR = {
				has_owner_culture = yes
				has_owner_accepted_culture = yes
			}
			OR = {
				culture_group = byzantine
				culture_group = iranian
				culture_group = egyptian_group
				culture_group = old_latin
				culture_group = latin
				culture = old_egyptian
				culture = al_misr_arabic
			}
		}
	}

	tier_0 = {
		#time to upgrade to this level (0 for tier 0)

			months = 0
		}

		}

		months = 120
	}
